<span style="font-family:'Helvetica-Light-Light-It';font-size:10.02pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3. </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">зӘҒз ҙй©ұеҠЁз№ҒиҚЈжңҹпјҲзәҰ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">21</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> дё–зәӘ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">10</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> е№ҙд»Јпјү</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Italic';font-size:9.48pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">Conversational speech transcription using context-dependent deep neural networks</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҢеұ•зӨәдәҶд»–д»¬еңЁж·ұ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еәҰзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңеә”з”ЁдәҺдјҡиҜқиҜӯйҹіиҪ¬еҪ•пјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Conversational Speech Transcription</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүйўҶеҹҹзҡ„зӘҒз ҙжҖ§е·ҘдҪңвҖ”вҖ”еңЁ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҚ•йҖҡйҒ“йқһзү№е®ҡдәәиҜӯйҹіиҜҶеҲ«пјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Single-Pass Speaker-Independent Recognition</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүеҹәеҮҶжөӢиҜ•ж–№йқўпјҢзӣёеҜ№й”ҷ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">иҜҜзҺҮз”ұ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">27.4%</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">йҷҚдҪҺеҲ°</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">18.5%</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҢзӣёеҜ№йҷҚе№…иҫҫ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">32%</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјӣеңЁе…¶д»–</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зұ»дёҚеҗҢд»»еҠЎдёӯпјҢд№ҹи§ӮеҜҹеҲ°</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">22%~28%</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">зҡ„</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">зӣёеҜ№й”ҷиҜҜзҺҮйҷҚдҪҺпјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Seide et al., 2011</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">дёҺж”ҫзҪ®д»ҘеҸҠйҖҡдҝЎеҚҸи°ғзӯ–з•Ҙд»ҘеҠ йҖҹи®ӯз»ғпјүпјҢиҜҘзі»з»ҹйғЁзҪІеңЁеӨҡеҸ°й…ҚзҪ®жңүиӢұдјҹиҫҫ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Tesla GPGPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зҡ„жңҚеҠЎ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҷЁдёҠпјҢйҖҡиҝҮж•°зҷҫе°Ҹж—¶зҡ„и®ӯз»ғжүҚе®ҢжҲҗгҖӮи®әж–ҮеңЁжңҖеҗҺиҮҙи°ўдёӯжҸҗеҲ°вҖң</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Our special thanks go to Ajith </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Jayamohan and Igor Kouzminykh of the MSR Extreme Computing Group for access to a Tesla server </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">farm, without which this work would not have been possible</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">вҖқпјҢз”ұжӯӨзңӢеҲ°еңЁ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> йўҶеҹҹз®—жі•еӣўйҳҹдёҺзі»з»ҹ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еӣўйҳҹеҚҸдҪңе·Із»Ҹз”ұжқҘе·Ід№…пјҢз®—жі•дёҺзі»з»ҹзҡ„еҚҸеҗҢи®ҫи®Ўе°Ҷд»ҘеҫҖдёҚеҸҜиғҪе®ҢжҲҗзҡ„и®Ўз®—д»»еҠЎеҸҳдёәдәҶеҸҜиғҪпјҢдёҠ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еұӮеә”з”ЁиҙҹиҪҪйңҖжұӮй©ұеҠЁзі»з»ҹеҸ‘еұ•дёҺжј”еҢ–пјҢзі»з»ҹж”Ҝж’‘дёҠеұӮеә”з”ЁиҙҹиҪҪеҸ–еҫ—ж–°зҡ„зӘҒз ҙгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">з§‘еӯҰе®¶йҖҡиҝҮиҝһжҺҘ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">16000</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> дёӘи®Ўз®—жңәеӨ„зҗҶеҷЁеҲӣе»әдәҶжңҖеӨ§зҡ„жңәеҷЁеӯҰд№ зҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңд№ӢдёҖпјҢд»–д»¬е°ҶиҝҷдәӣеӨ„зҗҶ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҷЁжқҫж•ЈеҲҶеёғеңЁдә’иҒ”зҪ‘дёҠиҮӘиЎҢеӯҰд№ пјҢжӯЈжҳҜиҝҷж ·еӨ§и§„жЁЎзі»з»ҹдә’иҒ”жӣҙеӨ§зҡ„з®—еҠӣж”Ҝж’‘дәҶзӣёжҜ”д»ҘеҫҖжӣҙеӨ§зҡ„</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">ж•°жҚ®йӣҶе’ҢжЁЎеһӢзҡ„и®ӯз»ғгҖӮжӯӨе·ҘдҪңи®әж–Ү</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Italic';font-size:9.48pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">Building high-level features using large scale unsupervised </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">2012</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> е№ҙ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жңҲпјҢ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Alex Krizhevsky</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">гҖҒ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Ilya Sutskever</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> е’Ң</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Geoffrey Hinton</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> еӣўйҳҹи®ҫи®Ўзҡ„</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AlexNet      </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҲеӣҫ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">1.1.8</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүиөўеҫ—дәҶ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">ImageNet</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> з«һиөӣпјҢж·ұеәҰзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңејҖе§ӢеҶҚж¬ЎжөҒиЎҢпјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Krizhevsky et al., 2012</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AlexNet</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">йҰ–ж¬Ўеј•е…ҘдәҶ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">ReLU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Rectified Linear Unit</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүжҝҖжҙ»еҮҪж•°пјҢе№¶жү©еұ•дәҶ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">LeNet5</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> з»“жһ„пјҢж·»еҠ дәҶ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Dropout</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> еұӮ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жқҘеҮҸе°ҸиҝҮжӢҹеҗҲпјҢж·»еҠ дәҶ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">LRN</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Local Response Normalization</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүеұӮжқҘеўһејәжіӣеҢ–иғҪеҠӣ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">/</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҮҸе°ҸиҝҮжӢҹеҗҲгҖӮ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">иҝҷдәӣж–°зҡ„жЁЎеһӢз»“жһ„е’Ңи®ӯз»ғж–№жі•еҪұе“ҚзқҖеҗҺз»ӯзҡ„жЁЎеһӢи®ҫи®Ўе’Ңзі»з»ҹдјҳеҢ–пјҢдҫӢеҰӮпјҢжҝҖжҙ»еҮҪж•°е’ҢеҚ·з§ҜеұӮзҡ„</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҶ…ж ёиһҚеҗҲи®Ўз®—зӯүгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AlexNet</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> йҮҮз”Ё</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> еқ—иӢұдјҹиҫҫ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">GTX 580 3 GB GPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> иҠұиҙ№</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пҪһ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> еӨ©е®ҢжҲҗи®ӯз»ғпјҢиӢҘжңүжӣҙ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҝ«зҡ„</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">GPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> е’ҢжӣҙеӨ§зҡ„ж•°жҚ®йӣҶпјҢ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AlexNet</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жңүжңӣеҫ—еҲ°жӣҙеҘҪзҡ„и®ӯз»ғз»“жһңгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">е•Ҷз”Ё</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">GPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> е’ҢеӨҡж¬ҫж¶Ҳиҙ№зә§</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">GPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҢиҝҷдәӣ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">GPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> е·Із»ҸејҖе§Ӣиў«з”ЁдәҺеҠ йҖҹ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> з®—жі•дёҺжЁЎеһӢзҡ„з ”з©¶пјҢиў«дёҡз•Ңе…¬</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҸёз”ЁдәҺдәәе·ҘжҷәиғҪдә§е“ҒгҖӮеҗҢж—¶пјҢд»Һ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AlexNet</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зҡ„е·ҘдҪңдёӯеҸҜд»ҘзңӢеҲ°пјҢз ”з©¶дәәе‘ҳеҹәдәҺ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">CUDA API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> иҝӣиЎҢзј–</span>

## Page 22

<span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">з¬¬1 з«   AI зі»з»ҹжҰӮиҝ° </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica-Light-Light-It';font-size:10.02pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">11</span><span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">1.2  AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> еҸ‘еұ•й©ұеҠЁеҠӣ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зҡ„иө·жәҗеҸҜиҝҪжәҜеҲ°</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">20</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> дё–зәӘ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">50</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> е№ҙд»ЈпјҢе…¶еҸ‘еұ•дёҖеәҰиө·иө·дјҸдјҸпјҢеҺҶз»ҸеӨҡж¬Ўз№ҒиҚЈдёҺдҪҺи°·пјҢзӣҙеҲ°</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">2016</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> е№ҙ</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AlphaGo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> иөўеҫ—дәҶдёҺдё–з•ҢеӣҙжЈӢеҶ еҶӣжқҺдё–зҹізҡ„жҜ”иөӣпјҢ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жүҚеңЁеӨ§дј—дёӯжҺҖиө·е№ҝжіӣзҡ„зғӯеәҰе’Ңе…іжіЁеәҰпјҢж Үеҝ—</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">зқҖ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> еҸ‘еұ•зҡ„ж–°дёҖиҪ®зғӯжҪ®гҖӮе…¶е®һпјҢ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жҠҖжңҜж—©еңЁиҝҷдёӘж Үеҝ—жҖ§дәӢд»¶д№ӢеүҚе°ұе·Із»ҸеңЁеҫҲеӨҡдә’иҒ”зҪ‘е…¬еҸёдёӯ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҫ—еҲ°дәҶе№ҝжіӣеә”з”ЁдёҺйғЁзҪІгҖӮдҫӢеҰӮпјҢжҗңзҙўеј•ж“ҺжңҚеҠЎдёӯзҡ„жҺ’еәҸгҖҒеӣҫеғҸзҡ„жЈҖзҙўгҖҒе№ҝе‘ҠжҺЁиҚҗзӯүеҠҹиғҪпјҢиғҢеҗҺ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">йғҪжңү</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жЁЎеһӢзҡ„ж”Ҝж’‘гҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">ж·ұеәҰеӯҰд№ жҠҖжңҜеҸ–еҫ—дәҶзӘҒз ҙжҖ§иҝӣеұ•пјҢжҳҜ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> дёӯжңҖдёәеүҚжІҝе’ҢйҮҚиҰҒзҡ„жҠҖжңҜпјҢе№¶дёҚж–ӯеңЁе№ҝжіӣзҡ„еә”з”ЁеңәжҷҜеҶ…</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҸ–д»Јдј з»ҹжңәеҷЁеӯҰд№ жЁЎеһӢгҖӮзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңжҳҜж·ұеәҰеӯҰд№ зҡ„е…·дҪ“е®һзҺ°еҪўжҖҒпјҢдҪҝз”ЁзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢжқҘиЎЁзӨәжңәеҷЁ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еӯҰд№ дёӯж·ұеәҰеӯҰд№ иҝҷдёҖиҢғејҸгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Bold';font-size:10.50pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000">1.2.1  AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> еӯҰд№ ж–№жі•</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Bold';font-size:10.50pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жҳҜеҰӮдҪ•е·ҘдҪңзҡ„гҖӮжң¬еҶ…е®№еҒҮе®ҡиҜ»иҖ…жңүдёҖе®ҡеҹәзЎҖпјҢзӣёе…іжҰӮеҝөжҡӮдёҚеңЁжң¬иҠӮиҝҮеӨҡи§ЈйҮҠгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҸҜд»Ҙи®ӨдёәпјҢжңәеҷЁеӯҰд№ жҳҜе®һзҺ°</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зҡ„дёҖз§Қж–№жі•пјҢиҖҢж·ұеәҰеӯҰд№ жҳҜе®һзҺ°жңәеҷЁеӯҰд№ зҡ„дёҖз§ҚжҠҖжңҜгҖӮеҪ“еүҚпјҢ</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">йүҙдәҺиҝҷж ·зҡ„е…ізі»пјҢеҗҺз»ӯзҡ„з« иҠӮдёӯпјҢе°Ҷдјҡд»Ҙ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> дёҖиҜҚд»ЈжҢҮзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңиҝҷдёҖе…·дҪ“е®һзҺ°еҪўжҖҒгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еңЁеұ•ејҖ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зі»з»ҹи®ҫи®Ўзӣёе…іеҶ…е®№д№ӢеүҚпјҢйңҖиҰҒйҰ–е…ҲдәҶи§Ј</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зҡ„еҺҹзҗҶдёҺзү№зӮ№гҖӮдёӢйқўе°Ҷд»Ҙе®һдҫӢд»Ӣз»Қ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">з»“еҗҲеӣҫ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">1.2.1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҢж·ұеәҰзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңзҡ„ејҖеҸ‘дёҺе·ҘдҪңжЁЎејҸеҸҜд»ҘжҰӮжӢ¬дёәд»ҘдёӢеҮ дёӘжӯҘйӘӨпјҡ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:7.98pt;color:#000000">еӣҫ1.2.1 </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">в—Ҹ </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">зЎ®е®ҡжЁЎеһӢиҫ“е…Ҙиҫ“еҮәпјҡйҰ–е…ҲйңҖиҰҒзЎ®и®ӨзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢзҡ„иҫ“е…Ҙж ·жң¬пјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Sample</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүе’Ңиҫ“еҮәж Үзӯҫ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жў…гҖҒй©¬з»ҝжў…пјүгҖӮз”ЁжҲ·йңҖиҰҒжҸҗеүҚеҮҶеӨҮеҘҪжЁЎеһӢзҡ„иҫ“е…Ҙиҫ“еҮәж•°жҚ®пјҢиҝӣиҖҢеұ•ејҖеҗҺз»ӯзҡ„жЁЎеһӢи®ӯз»ғгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">в—Ҹ </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">и®ҫи®ЎдёҺејҖеҸ‘жЁЎеһӢпјҡејҖеҸ‘иҖ…йҖҡиҝҮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жЎҶжһ¶жҸҗдҫӣзҡ„</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> ејҖеҸ‘зҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢгҖӮеңЁзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢз»“</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Label</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүгҖӮдҫӢеҰӮпјҢеӣҫ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">1.2.1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> дёӯеҗ‘жЁЎеһӢиҫ“е…ҘеӣҫзүҮпјҢиҫ“еҮәеӣҫзүҮжүҖеҜ№еә”зҡ„зұ»еҲ«пјҲй©¬еҶ¬жў…гҖҒй©¬е°Ҹжў…гҖҒй©¬зәў</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 23

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica-Light-Light-It';font-size:10.02pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">12</span><span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">AI зі»з»ҹпјҡеҺҹзҗҶдёҺжһ¶жһ„ </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жһ„зҡ„еҹәжң¬иЎЁзӨәдёӯпјҢдёҖиҲ¬зәҝж®өпјҲиҝһзәҝпјүд»ЈиЎЁжқғйҮҚпјҢеңҶеңҲд»ЈиЎЁиҫ“е…Ҙж•°жҚ®еҸ‘з”ҹеҸҳеҢ–зҡ„е…·дҪ“и®Ўз®—ж“ҚдҪңгҖӮ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">з®—жҜҸдёӘеұӮдёӯжҜҸдёӘжқғйҮҚе’ҢеҒҸе·®еҜ№жҖ»иҜҜе·®зҡ„иҙЎзҢ®пјҲжўҜеәҰ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">d</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Italic';font-size:9.48pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">l</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">/d</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Italic';font-size:9.48pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">w</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Italic';font-size:6.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">i</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүпјҢз„¶еҗҺдҪҝз”ЁжұӮи§ЈжўҜеәҰзҡ„дјҳеҢ–з®—жі•пјҲеҰӮ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еӣҫ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">1.2.2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> дёӯзҡ„жўҜеәҰдёӢйҷҚз®—жі•пјүеҺ»еҜ»жүҫж•°жҚ®зҡ„йһҚзӮ№пјҢд»ҺиҖҢеҜ№зҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢдјҳеҢ–жқғйҮҚеҸӮж•°е’ҢеҒҸе·®пјҢе№¶жңҖз»Ҳ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жңҖе°ҸеҢ–зҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңзҡ„жҖ»иҜҜе·®пјҲжҚҹеӨұеҖјпјҢеҚі</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Loss</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> еҖјпјүгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жў…еӣҫзүҮеҜ№еә”зҡ„вҖңй©¬еҶ¬жў…вҖқиҝҷдёӘзЎ®е®ҡжҖ§зҡ„иҫ“еҮәж Үзӯҫпјүзҡ„ж•°жҚ®йӣҶпјҢдёҚж–ӯйҖҡиҝҮдјҳеҢ–з®—жі•иҝӣиЎҢи®ӯз»ғеӯҰд№ гҖӮ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҰӮеҚ·з§ҜеұӮгҖҒжұ еҢ–еұӮзӯүпјүпјҢдә§з”ҹиҫ“еҮәе№¶е®ҢжҲҗжҚҹеӨұеҮҪж•°пјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Loss Function</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүи®Ўз®—гҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҜ№жҚҹеӨұеҮҪж•°зҡ„жўҜеәҰжұӮи§ЈгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жҢҮе®ҡеӯҰд№ зҺҮжӣҙж–°гҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">дёӘжҸҗеүҚи®ҫзҪ®зҡ„йҳҲеҖјпјүжҲ–иҫҫеҲ°з»ҲжӯўжқЎд»¶пјҲдҫӢеҰӮжҢҮе®ҡиҫҫеҲ°дёҖе®ҡиҝӯд»ЈпјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Step</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүж¬Ўж•°з„¶еҗҺеҒңжӯўи®ӯз»ғпјүгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">и¶ійңҖжұӮзҡ„йў„жөӢж•ҲжһңгҖӮеҰӮжһңејҖеҸ‘иҖ…еҜ№жЁЎеһӢйў„жөӢж•Ҳжһңж»Ўж„ҸпјҢе°ұеҸҜд»Ҙиҝӣе…ҘжЁЎеһӢйғЁзҪІиҝӣиЎҢжҺЁзҗҶе’ҢдҪҝз”ЁжЁЎ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еһӢгҖӮдёҖеҸҘиҜқиҖҢиЁҖпјҢжҲ‘д»¬и®ӯз»ғ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жЁЎеһӢзҡ„иҝҮзЁӢпјҢе°ұжҳҜйҖҡиҝҮдёҚж–ӯең°иҝӯд»Ји®Ўз®—пјҢдҪҝз”ЁжўҜеәҰдёӢйҷҚзҡ„дјҳеҢ–з®—</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">е…¶дёӯпјҢжқғйҮҚз”Ё</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Italic';font-size:9.48pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">w</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Italic';font-size:6.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">i</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> иЎЁзӨәпјҢжҳҜеҸҜд»Ҙиў«еӯҰд№ е’ҢдёҚж–ӯжӣҙж–°зҡ„ж•°еҖјпјҢз®Җз§°дёәзҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢзҡ„еҸӮж•°гҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">в—Ҹ </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">и®ӯз»ғпјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman,Bold';font-size:9.48pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000">Training</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүиҝҮзЁӢпјҡи®ӯз»ғзҡ„жң¬иҙЁжҳҜйҖҡиҝҮзҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢдёӯзҡ„иҝһжҺҘйҖҗеұӮеҸҚеҗ‘дј ж’ӯжҖ»иҜҜе·®пјҢи®Ў</span>

## Page 25

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica-Light-Light-It';font-size:10.02pt;font-style:italic;color:#000000">14</span><span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXH1K--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">AI зі»з»ҹпјҡеҺҹзҗҶдёҺжһ¶жһ„ </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">дёӢйқўз®ҖиҰҒеҪ’зәіеҮ з§Қжңүд»ЈиЎЁжҖ§зҡ„</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">AI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> жЁЎеһӢз»“жһ„пјҡ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">дёәдё»пјҢжұ еҢ–еұӮпјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Pooling Layer</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүгҖҒе…ЁиҝһжҺҘеұӮпјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Fully Connected Layer</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүзӯүз®—еӯҗпјҲ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Operator</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүз»„еҗҲеҪў</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жҲҗзҡ„зҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңжЁЎеһӢгҖӮе…¶еңЁ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">CV</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> йўҶеҹҹеҸ–еҫ—жҳҺжҳҫж•Ҳжһңе’Ңе№ҝжіӣеә”з”ЁгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">Short-Term Memory</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјҢ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">LSTM</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">пјүзӯүеҹәжң¬еҚ•е…ғз»„еҗҲеҪўжҲҗзҡ„йҖӮеҗҲж—¶еәҸж•°жҚ®йў„жөӢпјҲдҫӢеҰӮпјҢиҮӘз„¶иҜӯиЁҖеӨ„зҗҶгҖҒ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">иҜӯйҹіиҜҶеҲ«гҖҒзӣ‘жҺ§ж—¶еәҸж•°жҚ®зӯүпјүзҡ„жЁЎеһӢз»“жһ„гҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">з®—жі•жҖ»з§°гҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">GNN</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> зҡ„зӣ®зҡ„жҳҜе°ҪеҸҜиғҪеӨҡең°жҸҗеҸ–</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">вҖңеӣҫвҖқ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">дёӯжҪңеңЁзҡ„иЎЁеҫҒдҝЎжҒҜгҖӮ</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҸҳеҲҶдј°и®Ўи®ӯз»ғзҡ„й©¬е°”еҸҜеӨ«й“ҫгҖӮиҜҘжЁЎеһӢзҡ„зӣ®ж ҮжҳҜйҖҡиҝҮеҜ№ж•°жҚ®зӮ№еңЁжҪңз©әй—ҙдёӯзҡ„жү©ж•Јж–№ејҸиҝӣиЎҢе»әжЁЎпјҢ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">жқҘеӯҰд№ ж•°жҚ®йӣҶзҡ„жҪңз»“жһ„гҖӮдҫӢеҰӮпјҢе…¶еңЁи®Ўз®—жңәи§Ҷи§үдёӯпјҢйҖҡиҝҮеӯҰд№ йҖҶжү©ж•ЈиҝҮзЁӢи®ӯз»ғзҘһз»ҸзҪ‘з»ңпјҢд»ҺиҖҢ</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">еҜ№еҸ еҠ дәҶй«ҳж–ҜеҷӘеЈ°зҡ„еӣ
